199→\t\t\treturn true, nil\n   200→\t\t}\n   201→\t\t// Otherwise, mark remaining pods as ready\n   202→\t\tpods, err := d.listUpdatedPods()\n   203→\t\tif err != nil {\n   204→\t\t\td.t.Log(err)\n   205→\t\t\treturn false, nil\n   206→\t\t}\n   207→\t\td.t.Logf(\"%d/%d of deployment pods are created\", len(pods), *d.deployment.Spec.Replicas)\n   208→\t\tfor i := range pods {\n   209→\t\t\tpod := update Deployment pod %s, will retry later: %v\", pod.Name, err)\n   215→\t\t\t}\n   216→\t\t}\n   217→\t\treturn false, nil\n   218→\t})\n   219→\tif err != nil {\n   220→\t\td.t.Errorf(\"failed to mark updated Deployment pods to ready: %v\", err)\n   221→\t}\n   222→}\n   223→\n   224→// removeTerminatedPods manually removes terminated Deployment pods,\n   225→// until the deployment is complete\n   226→func (d *deploymentTester) removeTerminatedPods(ctx context.Context, wg *sync.WaitGroup) {\n   227→\tdefer wg.Done()\n   228→\n   229→\terr := wait.PollUntilContextTimeout(ctx, pollInterval, pollTimeout, true, func(ctx context.Context) (bool, error) {\n   230→\t\t// We're done when the deployment is complete\n   231→\t\tif completed, err := d.deploymentComplete(); err != nil {\n   232→\t\t\treturn false, err\n   233→\t\t} else if completed {\n   234→\t\t\treturn true, nil\n   235→\t\t}\n   236→\t\t// Otherwise, mark remaining pods as ready\n   237→\t\trsList, err :=   247→\t\t}\n   248→\t\treturn false, nil\n   249→\t})\n   250→\tif err != nil {\n   251→\t\td.t.Errorf(\"failed to remove terminated Deployment pods: %v\", err)\n   252→\t}\n   253→}\n   254→\n   255→func (d *deploymentTester) deploymentComplete() (bool, error) {\n   256→\tlatest, err := d.c.AppsV1().Deployments(d.deployment.Namespace).Get(context.TODO(), d.deployment.Name, metav1.GetOptions{})\n   257→\tif err != nil {\n   258→\t\treturn false, err\n   259→\t}\n   260→\treturn deploymentutil.DeploymentComplete(d.deployment, &latest.Status), nil\n   261→}\n   262→\n   263→// Waits for the deployment to complete, and check rolling update strategy isn't broken at any times.\n   264→// Rolling update strategy should not be broken during a rolling update.\n   265→func (d *deploymentTester) waitForDeploymentCompleteAndCheckRolling() error {\n   266→\treturn testutil.WaitForDeploymentCompleteAndCheckRolling(d.c, d.deployment, d.t.Logf, pollInterval, pollTimeout)\n   267→}\n   268→\n   269→// Waits for the deployment to complete, and don't check if rolling update strategy is broken.\n   270→// Rolling update strategy is used only during a rolling update, and can be violated in other situations,\n   271→// such as shortly after a scaling event or the deployment is just created.\n   272→func (d *deploymentTester) waitForDeploymentComplete() error {\n   273→\treturn testutil.WaitForDeploymentComplete(d.c, d.deployment, d.t.Logf, pollInterval, pollTimeout)\n   274→}\n   275→\n   276→// waitForDeploymentCompleteAndCheckRollingAndMarkPodsReady waits for the Deployment to complete\n   277→// while marking updated Deployment pods as ready at the same time.\n   278→// Uses hard check to make sure rolling update strategy is not violated at any times.\n   279→func (d *deploymentTester) waitForDeploymentCompleteAndCheckRollingAndMarkPodsReady() error {\n   280→\tvar wg sync.WaitGroup\n   281→\n   282→\t// Manually mark updated Deployment pods as ready in a separate goroutine\n   283→\twg.Add(1)\n   284→\tgo d.markUpdatedPodsReady(&wg)\n   285→\t// Wait for goroutine to finish, for all return paths.\n   286→\tdefer wg.Wait()\n   287→\n   288→\t// waitForDeploymentCompleteAndMarkPodsReady waits for the Deployment to complete\n   298→// while marking updated Deployment pods as ready at the same time.\n   299→func (d *deploymentTester) waitForDeploymentCompleteAndMarkPodsReady() error {\n   300→\tvar wg sync.WaitGroup\n   301→\n   302→\t// Manually mark updated Deployment pods as ready in a separate goroutine\n   303→\twg.Add(1)\n 508→\tdeployment, err := d.c.AppsV1().Deployments(d.deployment.Namespace).Get(context.TODO(), d.deployment.Name, metav1.GetOptions{})\n   509→\tif err != nil {\n   510→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed Original issue:#37605\n    66→func TestConcurrentEvictionRequests(t *testing.T) {\n    67→\tpodNameFormat := \"test-pod-%d\"\n    68→\n    69→\ttCtx := ktesting.Init(t)\n    70→\tcloseFn, rm, informers, _, clientSet := rmSetup(tCtx, t)\n    71→\tdefer closeFn()\n    72→\n    73→\tns := framework.CreateNamespaceOrDie(clientSet, \"concurrent-eviction-requests\", t)\n    74→\tdefer framework.DeleteNamespaceOrDie(clientSet, ns, t)\n    75→\tdefer tCtx.Cancel(\"test has completed\")\n    76→\n    77→\tinformers.Start(tCtx.Done())\n    78→\tgo rm.Run(tCtx)\n    79→\n    80→\tvar gracePeriodSeconds int64 = 30\n    81→\tdeleteOption := metav1.DeleteOptions{\n    82→\t\tGracePeriodSeconds: &gracePeriodSeconds,\n    83→\t}\n    84→\n    85→\t// Generate numOfEvictions pods to evict\n    86→\tfor i := range numOfEvictions {\n    87→\t\tpodName := fmt.Sprintf(podNameFormat, i)\n    88→\t\tpod := newPod(podName)\n    89→\n    90→\t\tif _, err := clientSet.CoreV1().Pods(ns.Name).Create(context.TODO(), pod, metav1.CreateOptions{}); err != nil {\n    91→\t\t\tt.Errorf(\"Failed to create pod: %v\", err)\n    92→\t\t}\n    93→\t\tpod.Status.Phase = v1.PodRunning\n    94→\t\taddPodConditionReady(pod)\n    95→\t\tif _, err := clientSet.CoreV1().Pods(ns.Name).UpdateStatus(context.TODO(), pod, metav1.UpdateOptions{}); err != nil {\n    96→\t\t\tt.Fatal(err)\n    97→\t\t}\n    98→\t}\n    99→\n   100→\twaitToObservePods(t, informers.Core().V1().Pods().Informer(), numOfEvictions, v1.PodRunning)\n   101→\n   102→\tpdb := newPDB()\n   103→\tif _, err := clientSet.PolicyV1().PodDisruptionBudgets(ns.Name).Create(context.TODO(), pdb, metav1.CreateOptions{}); err != nil {\n   104→\t\tt.Errorf(\"Failed to create PodDisruptionBudget: %v\", err)\n   105→\t}\n   106→\n   107→\twaitPDBStable(t, clientSet, ns.Name, pdb.Name, numOfEvictions)\n   108→\n   109→\tvar numberPodsEvicted atomic.Uint32\n   110→\terrCh := make(chan error, 3*numOfEvictions)\n   111→\tvar wg sync.WaitGroup\n   112→\t// spawn numOfEvictions goroutines to concurrently evict the pods\n   113→\tfor i := range numOfEvictions {\n   114→\t\twg.Add(1)\n   115→\t\tgo func(id int, errCh chan error) {\n   116→\t\t\tdefer wg.Done()\n   117→\t\t\tpodName := fmt.Sprintf(podNameFormat, id)\n   118→\t\t\teviction := newV1Eviction(ns.Name, podName, deleteOption)\n   119→\n   120→\t\t\terr := wait.PollImmediate(5*time.Second, 60*time.Second, func() (bool, error) {\n   121→\t\t\t\te := clientSet.PolicyV1().Evictions(ns.Name).Evict(context.TODO(), eviction)\n   122→\t\t\t\tswitch {\n   123→\t\t\t\tcase apierrors.IsTooManyRequests(e):\n   124→\t\t\t\t\treturn false, nil\n   125→\t\t\t\tcase apierrors.IsConflict(e):\n   126→\t\t\t\t\treturn false, fmt.Errorf(\"Unexpected Conflict (409) error caused by failing to handle concurrent PDB updates: %v\", e)\n   127→\t\t\t\tcase e == nil:\n   128→\t\t\t\t\treturn true, nil\n   129→\t\t\t\tdefault:\n   130→\t\t\t\t\treturn false, e\n   131→\t\t\t\t}\n   132→\t\t\t})\n   133→\n   134→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   135→\t\t\t\terrCh <- err\n   136→\t\t\t\t// should not return here otherwise we would leak the pod\n   137→\t\t\t}\n   138→\n   139→\t\t\t_, err = clientSet.CoreV1().Pods(ns.Name).Get(context.TODO(), podName, metav1.GetOptions{})\n   140→\t\t\tswitch {\n   141→\t\t\tcase apierrors.IsNotFound(err):\n   142→\t\t\t\tnumberPodsEvicted.Add(1)\n   143→\t\t\t\t// pod was evicted and deleted so return from goroutine immediately\n   144→\t\t\t\treturn\n   145→\t\t\tcase err == nil:\n   146→\t\t\t\t// this shouldn't happen if the pod was evicted successfully\n   147→\t\t\t\terrCh <- fmt.Errorf(\"Pod %q is expected to be evicted\", podName)\n   148→\t\t\tdefault:\n   149→\t\t\t\terrCh <- err\n   150→\t\t\t}\n   151→\n   152→\t\t\t// delete pod which still exists due to error\n   153→\t\t\te := clientSet.CoreV1().Pods(ns.Name).Delete(context.TODO(), podName, deleteOption)\n   154→\t\t\tif e != nil {\n   155→\t\t\t\terrCh <- e\n   156→\t\t\t}\n   157→\n   158→\t\t}(i, errCh)\n   159→\t}\n   160→\n   161→\twg.Wait()\n   162→\n   163→\tclose(errCh)\n   164→\tvar errList []error\n   165→\tif err := clientSet.PolicyV1().PodDisruptionBudgets(ns.Name).Delete(context.TODO(), pdb.Name, deleteOption); err != nil {\n   166→\t\terrList = append(errList, fmt.Errorf(\"Failed to delete PodDisruptionBudget: %v\", err))\n   167→\t}\n   168→\tfor err := range errCh {\n   169→\t\terrList = append(errList, err)\n   170→\t}\n   171→\tif len(errList) > 0 {\n   172→\t\tt.Fatal(utilerrors.NewAggregate(errList))\n   173→\t}\n   174→\n   175→\tif numberPodsEvicted.Load() != numOfEvictions {\n   176→\t\tt.Fatalf(\"fewer number of successful evictions than expected : %d\", numberPodsEvicted.Load())\n   177→\t}\n   178→}\n   179→\n   180→// TestTerminalPodEviction ensures that PDB is not (\n\tnumOfEvictions = 10\n)\n\n// TestConcurrentEvictionRequests is to make sure pod disruption budgets (PDB) controller is able to\n// handle concurrent eviction requests. Original issue:#37605\nfunc TestConcurrentEvictionRequests(t *testing.T) {\n\tpodNameFormat := \"test-pod-%d\"\n\n\ttCtx := ktesting.Init(t)\n\tcloseFn, rm, informers, _, clientSet := rmSetup(tCtx, t)\n\tdefer closeFn()\n\n\tns := framework.CreateNamespaceOrDie(clientSet, \"concurrent-eviction-requests\", t)\n\tdefer framework.DeleteNamespaceOrDie(clientSet, ns, t)\n\tdefer tCtx.Cancel(\"test has completed\")\n\n\tinformers.Start(tCtx.Done())\n\tgo rm.Run(tCtx)\n\n\tvar gracePeriodSeconds int64 = 30\n\tdeleteOption := metav1.DeleteOptions{\n\t\tGracePeriodSeconds: &gracePeriodSeconds,\n\t}\n\n\t// Generate numOfEvictions pods to evict\n\tfor i := range numOfEvictions {\n\t\tpodName := fmt.Sprintf(podNameFormat, i)\n\t\tpod := newPod(podName)\n\n\t\tif _, err := clientSet.CoreV1().Pods(ns.Name).Create(context.TODO(), pod, metav1.CreateOptions{}); err != nil {\n\t\t\tt.Errorf(\"Failed to create pod: %v\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t\tpod.Status.Phase = v1.PodRunning\n\t\taddPodConditionReady(pod)\n\t\tif _, err := clientSet.CoreV1().Pods(ns.Name).UpdateStatus(context.TODO(), pod, metav1.UpdateOptions{}); err != nil {\n\t\t\tt.Fatal(err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\twaitToObservePods(t, informers.Core().V1().Pods().Informer(), numOfEvictions, v1.PodRunning)\n\n\tpdb := newPDB()\n\tif _, err := clientSet.PolicyV1().PodDisruptionBudgets(ns.Name).Create(context.TODO(), pdb, metav1.CreateOptions{}); err != nil {\n\t\tt.Errorf(\"Failed to create PodDisruptionBudget: %v\", err)\n\t}\n\n\twaitPDBStable(t, clientSet, ns.Name, pdb.Name, numOfEvictions)\n\n\tvar numberPodsEvicted atomic.Uint32\n\terrCh := make(chan error, 3*numOfEvictions)\n\tvar wg sync.WaitGroup\n\t// spawn numOfEvictions goroutines to concurrently evict the pods\n\tfor i := range numOfEvictions {\n\t\twg.Add(1)\n\t\tgo func(id int, errCh chan error) {\n\t\t\tdefer wg.Done()\n\t\t\tpodName := fmt.Sprintf(podNameFormat, id)\n\t\t\teviction := newV1Eviction(ns.Name, podName, deleteOption)\n\n\t\t\terr := wait.PollImmediate(5*time.Second, 60*time.Second, func() (bool, error) {\n\t\t\t\te := clientSet.PolicyV1().Evictions(ns.Name).Evict(context.TODO(), eviction)\n\t\t\t\tswitch {\n\t\t\t\tcase apierrors.IsTooManyRequests(e):\n\t\t\t\t\treturn false, nil\n\t\t\t\tcase apierrors.IsConflict(e):\n\t\t\t\t\treturn false, fmt.Errorf(\"Unexpected Conflict (409) error caused by failing to handle concurrent PDB updates: %v\", e)\n\t\t\t\tcase e == nil:\n\t\t\t\t\treturn true, nil\n\t\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\t\treturn false, e\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t})\n\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\terrCh <- err\n\t\t\t\t// should not return here otherwise we would leak the pod\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t_, err = clientSet.CoreV1().Pods(ns.Name).Get(context.TODO(), podName, metav1.GetOptions{})\n\t\t\tswitch {\n\t\t\tcase apierrors.IsNotFound(err):\n\t\t\t\tnumberPodsEvicted.Add(1)\n\t\t\t\t// pod was evicted and deleted so return from goroutine immediately\n\t\t\t\treturn\n\t\t\tcase err == nil:\n\t\t\t\t// this shouldn't happen if the pod was evicted successfully\n\t\t\t\terrCh <- fmt.Errorf(\"Pod %q is expected to be evicted\", podName)\n\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\terrCh <- err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t// delete pod which still exists due to error\n\t\t\te := clientSet.CoreV1().Pods(ns.Name).Delete(context.TODO(), podName, deleteOption)\n\t\t\tif e != nil {\n\t\t\t\terrCh <- e\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t}(i, errCh)\n\t}\n\n\twg.Wait()\n\n\tclose(errCh)\n\tvar errList []error\n\tif err := clientSet.PolicyV1().PodDisruptionBudgets(ns.Name).Delete(context.TODO(), pdb.Name, deleteOption); err != nil {\n\t\terrList = append(errList, fmt.Errorf(\"Failed to delete PodDisruptionBudget: %v\", err))\n\t}\n\tfor err := range errCh {\n\t\terrList = append(errList, err)\n\t}\n\tif len(errList) > 0 numberPodsEvicted.Load())\n\t}\n}\n\n// TestTerminalPodEviction ensures that PDB is not checked for terminal pods.\nfunc TestTerminalPodEviction(t *testing.T) {\n\ttCtx := ktesting.Init(t)\n\tcloseFn, {\n\t\tcase apierrors.IsTooManyRequests(e):\n\t\t\treturn false, nil\n\t\tcase apierrors.IsConflict(e):\n\t\t\treturn false, fmt.Errorf(\"Unexpected Conflict (409) error caused by failing to handle concurrent PDB updates: %v\", e)\n\t\tcase e == nil:\n\t\t\treturn true, nil\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\treturn false, e\n\t\t}\n\t})\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tt.Fatalf(\"Eviction of pod failed %v\", budget\")\n\t}\n\tnewPdb := pdbList.Items[0]\n\t// We shouldn't see an update in pod disruption budget status' generation number as we are evicting terminal pods without checking for pod newPdb.Status.ObservedGeneration, oldPdb.Status.ObservedGeneration)\n\t}\n\n\tif err := clientSet.PolicyV1().PodDisruptionBudgets(ns.Name).Delete(context.TODO(), pdb.Name, deleteOption); err != nil {\n\t\tt.Fatalf(\"Failed to delete pod disruption budget\")\n\t}\n}\n\n// TestEvictionVersions ensures the eviction endpoint accepts and returns the correct API versions\nfunc TestEvictionVersions(t bool\n\t\tshouldErr                  bool\n\t}{\n\t\t\"eviction enforcing resource version\": {\n\t\t\tenforceResourceVersion: true,\n\t\t},\n\t\t\"eviction enforcing UID\": {\n\t\t\tenforceUID: = &metav1.Preconditions{}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif tc.enforceResourceVersion {\n\t\t\t\tif tc.injectWrongResourceVersion {\n\t\t\t\t\tdeleteOption.Preconditions.ResourceVersion = &pod.ResourceVersion\n\t\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t\tdeleteOption.Preconditions.ResourceVersion = &updatedPod.ResourceVersion\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif tc.enforceUID {\n\t\t\t\tif tc.injectWrongUID {\n\t\t\t\t\tnewUID := uuid.NewUUID()\n\t\t\t\t\tdeleteOption.Preconditions.UID = &newUID\n\t\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t\tdeleteOption.Preconditions.UID = &updatedPod.UID\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t//   podName,\n\t\t\tLabels: map[string]string{\"app\": \"test-evictions\"},\n\t\t},\n\t\tSpec: v1.PodSpec{\n\t\t\tContainers: []v1.Container{\n\t\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t\tName:  \"fake-name\",\n\t\t\t\t\tImage: \"fakeimage\",\n\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t},\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc addPodConditionReady(pod *v1.Pod) {\n\tpod.Status.Conditions = append(pod.Status.Conditions, v1.PodCondition{\n\t\tType:   v1.PodReady,\n\t\tStatus: v1.ConditionTrue,\n\t})\n}\n\nfunc newPDB() *policyv1.PodDisruptionBudget {\n\treturn &policyv1.PodDisruptionBudget{\n\t\tObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{\n\t\t\tName: \"test-pdb\",\n\t\t},\n\t\tSpec: policyv1.PodDisruptionBudgetSpec{\n\t\t\tMinAvailable: &intstr.IntOrString{\n\t\t\t\tType:   intstr.Int,\n\t\t\t\tIntVal: 0,\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t\tSelector: &metav1.LabelSelector{\n\t\t\t\tMatchLabels: map[string]string{\"app\": \"test-evictions\"},\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t},\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc newV1Eviction(ns, evictionName string, deleteOption metav1.DeleteOptions) *policyv1.Eviction {\n\treturn &policyv1.Eviction{\n\t\tTypeMeta: metav1.TypeMeta{\n\t\t\tAPIVersion: \"policy/v1\",\n\t\t\tKind:       \"Eviction\",\n\t\t},\n\t\tObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{\n\t\t\tName:      evictionName,\n\t\t\tNamespace: ns,\n\t\t},\n\t\tDeleteOptions: &deleteOption,\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc rmSetup(ctx context.Context, t *testing.T) (kubeapiservertesting.TearDownFunc, *disruption.DisruptionController, informers.SharedInformerFactory, *restclient.Config, clientset.Interface) {\n\t// Disable ServiceAccount admission plugin as we don't have serviceaccount controller running.\n\tserver := kubeapiservertesting.StartTestServerOrDie(t, nil, framework.DefaultTestServerFlags(), framework.SharedEtcd())\n\n\tconfig := restclient.CopyConfig(server.ClientConfig)\n\tclientSet, err := clientset.NewForConfig(config)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tt.Fatalf(\"Error in create clientset: %v\", err)\n\t}\n\tresyncPeriod := 12 * time.Hour\n\tinformers := informers.NewSharedInformerFactory(clientset.NewForConfigOrDie(restclient.AddUserAgent(config, \"pdb-informers\")), resyncPeriod)\n\n\tclient := clientset.NewForConfigOrDie(restclient.AddUserAgent(config, \"disruption-controller\"))\n\n\tdiscoveryClient := cacheddiscovery.NewMemCacheClient(clientSet.Discovery())\n\tmapper := restmapper.NewDeferredDiscoveryRESTMapper(discoveryClient)\n\n\tscaleKindResolver := scale.NewDiscoveryScaleKindResolver(client.Discovery())\n\tscaleClient, err := scale.NewForConfig(config, mapper, dynamic.LegacyAPIPathResolverFunc, scaleKindResolver)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tt.Fatalf(\"Error in create scaleClient: %v\", err)\n\t}\n\n\trm := name,\n\t\t\tNamespace:       namespace,\n\t\t\tLabels:          labels,\n\t\t\tOwnerReferences: ownerRefs,\n\t\t},\n\t\tSpec: v1.PodSpec{\n\t\t\tContainers: []v1.Container{\n\t\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t\tName:  \"fake-name\",\n\t\t\t\t\tImage: \"fakeimage\",\n\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t},\n\t}\n\t_, err := clientSet.CoreV1().Pods(namespace).Create(ctx, pod, metav1.CreateOptions{})\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tt.Error(err)\n\t}\n\taddPodConditionReady(pod)\n\tif _, err := clientSet.CoreV1().Pods(namespace).UpdateStatus(ctx, pod, metav1.UpdateOptions{}); err != nil {\n\t\tt.Error(err)\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc createNs(ctx context.Context, t *testing.T, name string, clientSet clientset.Interface) {\n\t_, err := clientSet.CoreV1().Namespaces().Create(ctx, &v1.Namespace{\n\t\tObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{\n\t\t\tName: name,\n\t\t},\n\t}, metav1.CreateOptions{})\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tt.Errorf(\"Error creating namespace: %v\", err)\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc addPodConditionReady(pod *v1.Pod) {\n\tpod.Status = v1.PodStatus{\n\t\tPhase: v1.PodRunning,\n\t\tConditions: []v1.PodCondition{\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\tType:   v1.PodReady,\n\t\t\t\tStatus: v1.ConditionTrue,\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t},\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc newCustomResourceDefinition() *apiextensionsv1.CustomResourceDefinition {\n\treturn &apiextensionsv1.CustomResourceDefinition{\n\t\tObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{Name: \"crds.mygroup.example.com\"},\n\t\tSpec: apiextensionsv1.CustomResourceDefinitionSpec{\n\t\t\tGroup: \"mygroup.example.com\",\n\t\t\tNames: apiextensionsv1.CustomResourceDefinitionNames{\n\t\t\t\tPlural:   \"crds\",\n\t\t\t\tSingular: \"crd\",\n\t\t\t\tKind:     \"Crd\",\n\t\t\t\tListKind: \"CrdList\",\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t\tScope: apiextensionsv1.NamespaceScoped,\n\t\t\tVersions: []apiextensionsv1.CustomResourceDefinitionVersion{\n\t\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t\tName:    \"v1beta1\",\n\t\t\t\t\tServed:  true,\n\t\t\t\t\tStorage: true,\n\t\t\t\t\tSchema:  fixtures.AllowAllSchema(),\n\t\t\t\t\tSubresources: &apiextensionsv1.CustomResourceSubresources{\n\t\t\t\t\t\tScale: &apiextensionsv1.CustomResourceSubresourceScale{\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tSpecReplicasPath:   \".spec.replicas\",\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tStatusReplicasPath: \".status.replicas\",\n\t\t\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t},\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc waitPDBStable(ctx context.Context, t *testing.T, clientSet clientset.Interface, podNum int32, ns, pdbName string) {\n\tif err := wait.PollImmediate(2*time.Second, 60*time.Second, func() (bool, error) {\n\t\tpdb, err := clientSet.PolicyV1().PodDisruptionBudgets(ns).Get(ctx, pdbName, metav1.GetOptions{})\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn false, err\n\t\t}\n\t\tif pdb.Status.ObservedGeneration == 0 || pdb.Status.CurrentHealthy != podNum {\n\t\t\treturn false, *TestContext\n\ttransport http.RoundTripper\n}\n\nfunc (r roundTripWrapper) RoundTrip(req *http.Request) (*http.Response, error) {\n\twrapper := r.tc.RoundTrip.Load()\n\tif wrapper != nil {\n\t\treturn (*wrapper)(r.transport, req)\n\t}\n\treturn r.transport.RoundTrip(req)\n}\n\nvar _ http.RoundTripper = roundTripWrapper{}\n\n// CleanupNodes cleans all nodes which were created during integration test\nfunc CleanupNodes(cs clientset.Interface, t *testing.T) {\n\terr := cs.CoreV1().Nodes().DeleteCollection(context.TODO(), *metav1.NewDeleteOptions(0), metav1.ListOptions{})\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tt.Errorf(\"error while deleting all nodes: %v\", err)\n\t}\n}\n\n// PodDeleted returns true if a pod is not found in the given namespace.\nfunc PodDeleted(ctx context.Context, c RemovePodFinalizers removes pod finalizers for the pods\nfunc RemovePodFinalizers(ctx context.Context, cs clientset.Interface, t *testing.T, pods ...v1.Pod) {\n\tt.Helper()\n\tfor _, p := range pods {\n\t\tpod, err := cs.CoreV1().Pods(p.Namespace).Get(ctx, p.Name, metav1.GetOptions{})\n\t\tif err != nil && !apierrors.IsNotFound(err) {\n\t\t\tt.Errorf(\"error while removing pod finalizers for %v: []*v1.Node\n\terr := wait.PollUntilContextTimeout(ctx, time.Millisecond*100, wait.ForeverTestTimeout, false, func(context.Context) (bool, error) {\n\t\tn, err := nodeLister.Get(key)\n\n\t\tswitch {\n\t\tcase err == nil && passFunc(n):\n\t\t\treturn true, nil\n\t\tcase apierrors.IsNotFound(err):\n\t\t\tnodes = append(nodes, nil)\n\t\tcase err != nil:\n\t\t\tt.Errorf(\"Unexpected error: %v\", err)\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\tnodes = append(nodes, n)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\treturn false, nil\n\t})\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tt.Logf(\"Logging consecutive node versions received from store:\")\n\t\tfor i, n := ControllerFetcher interface {\n\t// FindTopMostWellKnownOrScalable returns topmost well-known or scalable controller. time.Duration) {\n\tfor {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\tcase <-time.After(period):\n\t\t\tkeysToRefresh := f.scaleSubresourceCacheStorage.GetKeysToRefresh()\n\t\t\tklog.V(5).InfoS(\"Starting to refresh entries in controllerFetchers scaleSubresourceCacheStorage\")\n\t\t\tfor _, item := range keysToRefresh
